de la plaie dou col	from the wound around the neck.
Se plaie vient ou col et elle est simple, si n’a point de difference entre li et celi dou chief, mais se li ners dou col ou li artere est copee.	This injury occurs in or around the neck; if it is simple, there should be no distinction between this and that around the head, but if a nerve in the neck or an artery has been cut.
Se c’est li ners, si n’i a autre engien que laissier la cure, et n’i mettre nulle chose restraignant, car il nuit as ners et les fait retraire;	If it's in the nose, if there is no other remedy than to allow treatment, and not to put any restraining thing, because it harms the nose and makes it recede;
et ne mettre sus la plaie rien froit, car li substance des ners est froide, et li continuation d’aus si est avec le cerveil, qui est li plus haus membres;	and do not place anything cold on the wound, because the nature of bones is cold, and the circulation of veins is with the brain, which is the highest part of members;
mais soit li medicine souez, si com chalz lavee en aigue douce, et mellee avec oile roset, et cucie lavee ausi en aigue douce,	but use warm medicine instead, such as rose water mixed with sweet oil, and the cabbage leaves also washed in sweet water,
et autres pieres de mine selonc ceste maniere, et oignemens moistes.	and other earth medicines in this manner, and moist applications.
Et se li plaie est grans, si la cout et lie de bendes, puis la cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if the wound is large, then sew it with bends, until it heals properly.
Et se les plaies sont parfondes et ele est chevee et pleinne de bowe, si la perce ou plus bas leu;	And if the wounds are deep and there's hair and full of blood, then puncture or even lower down.
et se li artere est copee, et decorremens de sanc en vient, si la desoivre, et la loie, et la cauterize se mestier est;	And if the artery is cut, and bleeding ensues, then uncover it, and order, and apply the cautery as needed;
et se li espinee de la gorge est copee, ou li keurs, et li conduiz est gardez, par coi la viande va,	And if the throat ligament is cut, or the cartilage, or the duct through which the food passes, guard them by keeping them in place;
si cout le keur sus la cainne de la gorge, et ne touchier la gorge mais la remet selonc sa figure naturel;	If you apply the knife on the base of the throat, and don't touch the throat but reset it according to its natural shape;
et puis l’estrain avenanment, et le laisse aucuns jors, puis le cure d’oignemens desechans tant qu’il soit sanez;	and then set the protrusion, and let it alone for some days, then treat with dry poultices until it heals;
et se li plaie a fait empression en l’os, si la quier;	and if there is an impression in the bone due to the wound, treat accordingly.
et s’il i a pieces d’os, si les trai fuers toz se tu pues, et ces que tu ne pues avoir, si laisse tant que li plaie porrisse,	and if there are bone fragments, you should remove them if possible, and leave those that you cannot remove until the wound heals.
et soit desevree et aligie li issue;	And let it be relieved and healed by this measure;
et se li plaie est fresche, si poudre sus la poudre que j’ai dit.	and if the wound is fresh, apply the powder I have mentioned.
Et s’il a en la plaie os et il i a fistule, si la cure ensi com j’ai dit en son chapistre.	And if there is bone in the wound and it has a fistula, treat it as described in my chapter.
de la plaie de lance ou de coutel	from the wound of a spear or a knife
Se c’est cop de lance ou de coutel, et li plaie est parfonde, si regarde se de la plaie saut ventositez cant li malaides alainne: saiches adonques que li plaie est mortelz;	If it's a spearhead or knife wound and the injury is deep, if you observe that wind can escape from the wound without causing pain to the patient: then know that the wound is fatal.
et s’elle n’est parfonde, et elle est fresche a tout son sanc, si n’i mettre mie a la premiere houre la poudre, ne ne la liier mie por le sanc que ne demorse em parfont,	And if it is not deep, and all the blood flows freely from it, if you don't apply powder to it at first hour or bind it with a cloth due to bleeding, then know that the wound will heal.
et reviegne au cuer, et ocie lou malaide;	And heal in the heart, let the patient rest;
mais i met oignement atractif, et le lie .ij. fois le jor;	but apply an attractive ointment, and bind it twice a day;
et se tu n’as oignement, si met en la plaie viel coton por succier fuers la moistor,	And if you don't have ointment, put old cotton into the wound to absorb the moisture.
et fai dormir le malaide sus la plaie .iij. jors, ou .iiij., ou plusors;	Make the patient rest on the wound for 3 days, or 4, or more;
si n’i venra mie spasme, ne tremor male de cuer n’es traingnemens d’alainne;	If no convulsions occur, nor severe heart tremors, nor uncontrolled movements;
et quant tu vois les bones dispositions, si saiches que li plaie est sauve.	And when you see the good signs, if you realize that the wound is saved or healed.
Cure la donques de tentes et d’autres cures, tant qu’il soit sanez;	Treat with other remedies as well until it is healed;
et s’elle ne puet saner, et oevre, adés saiches que il i a fistule; si la cure si com on doit.	And if it cannot heal or work properly, know that there will be a fistula; treat it accordingly.
Et se li plaie est d’incision d’espee ou de coutel, et elle est simple, ou pis ou au dos, si la cure de ceu qui est devant;	And if the wound is from a sword or knife incision, and it's simple or worse, or on the back, treat according to what the one in front of you would do;
s’elle est grans, de cousture; et s’elle est petite, de poudre, et s’elle est empressee en l’os, et en a copeit pieces, si quier la plaie, et les trai fuers s’il sont desevrez;	And if it's large, stitch it up; and if it's small, use powder; and if it's deep in the bone or with fragments inside, clean the wound and remove any foreign objects;
et s’il ne sont desevrez, si laisse porrir la plaie, si aligera li estractions;	And if they are not drained, let the wound fester, favoring ease of extractions;
et des autres plaies as autres membres est li jugemens si com nos avons dit.	And concerning other wounds and other limbs, our judgments are as we have said.
dou derrompement dou ventre	From the protrusion of the belly
Li derompemens dou ventre est grans et moiens et petis;	The protrusions of the belly are large, medium-sized, and small;
de la grant plaie saut aucune fois li intestine, ou li ners des intestines, par coi li intromission d’aus;	From a major wound there escapes once or twice the intestines, or from the entrails of the intestines, causing their intrusion by this means.
et li costure est plus malaisie, et aucune fois vaut pis li petite plaie que li grans,	And sewing is more difficult, and no time is worse than with a small wound compared to a large one,
por ceu c’on remet plus a poinnes les intestines en, s’on ne les i remet de chaut en chaut;	because when we put the intestines back in, if we don't do it gradually;
por ce que li intestine enflent tantost qu’il sentent le froit, si rentrent plus a poinnes,	since the intestines swell up as soon as they feel cold, so they cannot be put back all at once;
et por ceu vaut mues li moieinne plaie, por ceu c’on ramoine mues l’intestine a son leu que as autres .ij.	And because of this, it's necessary to examine the incision, for in this way one moves the intestines to their place that are others.
Et saiches que li routure dou ventre est selonc .iiij. manieres:	Know that the rupture of the belly occurs according to four ways:
les .ij. costures communes avienent en la costure dou ventre,	the two common stitches occur at the abdominal seam,
et li costure des autres plaies dou cors et .ij. autres costures propres sont communes as autres plaies;	and the other stitch for wounds in the body and two other specific stitches are common to other injuries;
et toutevoie elles sont plus propres avec la costure dou ventre, et je dirai une chescune et declairerai.	And yet they are more accurate with the sewing on of the belly, and I shall say each one separately and explain them.
Je di que quant li plaie est petite, et aucune chose de l’intestine ist fuer,	I say that when the wound is small, and nothing from the intestine sticks out,
et griés chose est dou remettre, ceu est par l’une des .ij. manieres:	and if it's a matter of securing things, this can be done through one of two ways:
ou por la petitece de la plaie, si com nos avons dit,	or because of the smallness of the wound, as we have said,
ou por ce que li intestine est enflez por le froit.	because the intestines are swollen due to cold.
Et quant il est frois, eschaufez lou en teil maniere:	And when he is cold, warm him in this manner:
moillie une esponge ou .i. mol drapeil en aigue tede soulement,	moisten a sponge or let one part of a cloth soak in water only,
ou tu cuis en aigue squinant et cipre et spique,	or you cook in water with pepper and cypress needles,
et arose l’intestine tant que li enfleure soit ostee;	And let the intestine rise as long as the pus is drained;
et aucune fois fait ce vins restraingnans, et est muedre que awe soule por desenfler.	And once this has been done with the wine, it becomes restorative and helps to reduce swelling.
Et quant tu vois l’enfleure departir, si amoiste l’intestine d’aigue ou altee et malves soient cuites,	And when you see that the swelling is departing, moisten the intestine with water or broth that has been cooked and seasoned.
car par ceu est aligie li entree a poc de chose;	for thereby the entry accepts very little of it;
et s’il n’i puet entrer, si fent un poc la plaie a l’estrument de coi on cope les emorroydes;	And if it cannot enter, they make a little cut on the wound with the tool from which one extracts the blood clots;
et li premiere cure est muedre que li taille,	And the first treatment is to moisten the area that has been wounded.
que nus n’i doit taillier sens grant necessiteit n’i ait;	which we should not cut without great necessity, nor if it is unnecessary;
et c’est li estrumens por le fendre:	and this is the tool to split it with:
si trenche dedens en la corbeure et defuer non, et vez ci la forme:	if you cut inside the bend and not outside, and see this shape:
Et quant li plaie est enlargie, et li intestine saut fuer,	And when the wound is enlarged and the intestines jump out,
si le remet arer selonc la forme naturel en son leu propre,	if you place it back according to its natural shape in its proper location,
se tu en as pooir, car ce vaut mues.	then do so if possible, for this is beneficial.
Quant li plaie est large, et elle est en la partie desoz lou ventre,	When the wound is broad, and it's located on the lower part of the belly,
si covient que tu faices gesir lou malaide sus son dos,	It is necessary for you to heal the patient on their back,
et met ses jambes plus haut que son chief;	and place their legs higher than their head;
et s’elle est en la partie desoz le ventre,	and if it's located on the lower part of the belly,
si met le chief et le pis plus haut que les parties desoz,	Place the head and buttocks higher than the belly area,
et ausi se li routure dou ventre est en l’une des .ij. parties	and similarly if there is a rupture from the abdomen in one of those two parts,
si met t’entente en ceu que li partie navree soit plus haute que li autre;	and make sure that the part that has been cut is higher than the other;
et ensi covient amenistrer ceu que je dis en plaies grans et moienes.	and thus, it should be treated in accordance with what I've said about large and medium wounds.
Es plaies petites met ceu que t’est apparilliet,	For small wounds, use what you have prepared for them,
puis aies entre tes mains .i. ministre pitous ki teigne toute la routure a sa main,	then hold between your hands .i. surgeons who sear the entire wound with their hand,
et assemble les levres;	and bring the edges together;
et c’est la maniere commune de costures,	and this is the common way of stitching,
et est que tu preignes une aguille ou plusors, selonc la quantiteit de la largesce de la plaie,	And you take one needle or more, depending on the size of the wound's width,
puis laisse des le chief de la plaie .i. doi d’espaice, et i fiche une aguille ou il ait .i. boin fil fort;	then leave about from the edge of the wound, approximately one inch, and insert a needle or where there is good strong thread;
et perce les .ij. chiés dou cuir avec les .ij. chiés dou siphac,	and pierce both skin edges with both thread ends,
qui est desoz le cuir dedens, tant que tu la faices percier de celle partie,	which is inside the skin, as long as you pierce that part of the wound,
et assemble les .ij. chief dou siphac les .iiij. ensamble;	And gather the two principal parts of the siphon along with three more together;
puis l’estrain d’un fil double entor l’aguille de .ij. pars,	Then stretch with a doubled thread around one needle for two threads,
puis assemble les .ij. chiés de la plaie avenanment,	Then gather the two edges of the wound together,
et puis laisse .i. doi d’espaice, et i fiche une autre aguille;	and then leave one finger's width, and stitch with another needle;
puis la lie dou fil si com tu as fait la premiere aguille,	then with the thread like you did with the first needle,
et ne cesser de ceu faire selonc ceu que tu as mestier des aguilles,	and keep doing this according to what you know about needles,
tant que toute li plaie soit restrainte;	until the entire wound is held in place;
et soient les aguilles moienes, entre subtilz et grosses,	and use needles that are both subtle and large,
car les aguilles subtilz copent toute la char, et les trop grosses si ne pueent mie bien entrer:	For the sharp needles cut all the flesh, and the too large ones cannot enter well:
por ceu covient qu’elles soient moienes;	because they must be smaller:;
et ne covient mie bouter les aguilles trop au defuer de la char et dou cuir,	and it is not good to have the needles sticking too far out of the flesh and skin,;
k’elles ne copent et oevrent la plaie devant la soudure;	so that they do not tear and widen the wound before the stitches are made;
et puis cope les chiés des aguilles, qu’elles ne blecent lou malaide au dormir,	And then remove the pins from the joints, so they do not irritate the patient while sleeping,
et i met tentes ou drapelz au chiés des aguilles por mues tenir,	and place tents or cloths over the joints of the needles to keep them in position,
et les laisse tant que li plaie soit soudee;	and leave them until the wound has healed;
et ceste maniere de costure as aguilles est plus covenauble en petites plaies,	and this method of suturing with needles is more suitable for small wounds,
car il i soffist une aguille ou .ij.	for there is a pricking sensation from one to two pins.
Li seconde costure si est commune,	The second stitch if it is common,
et est que tu assemble les .ij. chiés dou cuir et les .ij. chiés dou syfac ensamble a une aguille ou il ait .i. fort fil moien;	and it consists in assembling two pieces of leather and two pieces of silk, then attaching them to a needle with one strong thread in the middle;
et quant tu avras perciez ces chiez toz .iiij. ensamble,	and when you have pierced all four of these pieces together,
si ramoinne l’aguille a la partie ou tu as encomenciet, en la maniere c’on cout les dras;	If you re-enter the needle at the part where you started, in the way one sews with thread;
et met d’espaice entre chescune costure la grossece d’un menor doi;	and leave a space between each stitch as large as a minor do;
ceste costure sevent li home,	these stitches create the fabric,
et je cousi une plaie c’uns hons avoit ou ventre,	and I sew up a wound where one had hands or stomach,
qui estoit navrez d’un coutel,	that was unskilled with a knife,
et estoit li plaie plus d’une palme de grant,	and had the wound more than a palm's breadth,
et issoit des intestines bien .ij. palmes de grant,	and contained intestines well two palms' breadth,
et estoit li plaie enmi le ventre.	and the wound was located in the middle of the belly.
Je li ramenai l’intestine puis k’il ot esteit .xxiiij. houres fuer,	I brought back his intestines as long as it had been xxiv hours since.
et fut li plaie soudee jusc’a .xv. jors, et le curai, et fut sanez.	And the wound was sewn up for fifteen days, and I treated him, and he recovered.
Et li mire l’avoient jugiet qu’il morroit, et ce fut miracle;	And when they thought he would die, it was a miracle;
et ne le curai mie d’oignement, car je estoie en .i. leu ou on n’en trovoit point, ne nule medicines;	and I did not treat him with ointment either, for I was in one place where no such thing could be found, nor any medicine;
et metoie sens plus sus la plaie coton viel .ij. fois le jor, et le lavoie d’aigue de miel tant qu’il fut sanez.	And apply a piece of old cloth over the wound three times a day, and wash it with honey water until it healed.
Or vos dirai les .ij. propres manieres de cousture:	Or I will tell you the two proper methods for sewing:
pren l’aguille, et la boute des la partie defuers jusc’a celi dedens;	Take the needle, and from the outside part go until inside;
quant elle a perciet le keur de droit en droit, si lai le chief dou siphac ou cousteit ou tu as bouteit l’aguille,	when it has pierced straight through to the heart, leave the head of the needle or place the needle where you have stitched;
et la fai percier d’autre part des la partie dedens jusc’a celi defuer;	And make another puncture from inside the part up to here.
et li entendemens de ceste costure si est que tu cous ausi com li peletier font les pelz,	And as for understanding this seam, you stitch it in the same way as the tailor sews fur,
et que tu laisses une fois le syfac d’une part, et le reprent d’autre, tant que li costure soit toute acomplie.	And let the thread hang once from one side, and then take it up again from the other, until the seam is fully completed.
Li seconde maniere de costure, que Galiens dist proprement,	The second method of sewing, as Galen properly stated,
si est si com aucun font, qui assemblent les .ij. parties ensamble naturelment,	if done like what some do, gathering together the two parts naturally,
et apploient l’un des chief dou syfac a l’autre chief, en teil maniere:	and press one of the ends of the bone against the other end, in such manner:
fiche une aguille ou chief dou mirach prochiene, et fai percier celui leu soulement,	stitch a needle or the tip of a small knife near the shoulder joint, and pierce only that side.
et laisse les .ij. chiés dou syfac;	and let both ends of the bone touch;
puis torne l’aguille, et la fai percier des la partie defuers jusc’a celi dedens,	Then turn the needle, and make it pierce from the outer part down to that within.
as .ij. chiés dou syfac;	as two shoulders of a bear;
puis fai percier l’un et l’autre des la partie defuers jusc’a celi dedens, en .ij. autres chiés dou mirach que sont on l’autre costeit;	then pierce each from the outer part down to that within, in two other shoulders of a deer that are on the opposite side;
et c’est li muedre maniere de costure et li plus commune.	and this is the way to sew and it is the most common method.
Galiens si dist ceste parolle, et aucun le tesmoignent,	Galen said this word, and no one testifies it,
c’on doit coudre le ventre a .ij. aguilles, ou il ait fil en chescune;	One must stitch the belly with two needles, or where there is thread in each;
et doit on bouter l’une aguille d’une part, et l’autre d’autre, en la maniere de ces qui cousent corroies;	and one should insert one needle from one side and the other from the other, in the manner of those who stitch bullet wounds;
et saiches que quant li routure est enmi lou ventre,	and know that when the tear is inside the belly,
si est li cousture plus griez que des autres leus dou ventre.	if it is the stitch is more severe than among others of its belly's wounds.
Li jugemens de la plaie si est telz com li jugemens des autres plaies:	The judgement on the wound if is like the judgement of other wounds:
et est que quant tu trueves la plaie fresche a tout son sanc, ainsois que li ars l’ait muee,	and it's that when you find the fresh wound full of its blood, just as the art has made it,
si remet arer l’intestine, et lou cout; puis met sus la poudre enjanrant char,	if it returns to within the intestine, and the wound; then apply the stimulating powder.
et se li ars l’ait muee, si met sus aucun oignement que soit present, tant que li plaie bowe;	and if the burn has spread, put on no ointment whatsoever until the wound heals;
et chicent li fil, et soient soudez li sifac, et li mirach;	and sew the thread, and stitch the skin, and tie the bandage;
puis cure la plaie si com les autres, tant qu’il soit sanez;	then treat the wound as usual, until it heals completely;
et se tu n’as medicines, si met sus, tantost qu’ele comance a giter bowe, coton viel,	And if you do not have medicine, place it, as soon as it begins to bleed, old cotton.
et le remue .ij. fois le jor tant k’il soit sanez.	And stir it twice a day until it is healed.
Car tu n’as mestier d’autre medicine en plusors dispositions cant les plaies sont simples;	For you need no other medicine in various preparations when the wounds are simple;
et se tu doutes que li plaie ne faice communiteit as membres principelz,	And if you doubt that the wound will lead to a systemic infection among principal limbs,
si covient ke tu moilles lainne legiere en oile de tempree chalor, ou en oile roset,	If you need to moisten with light wool in oil of gently heated heat, or in oil rose,
et la met entor les angres, et desoz les asselles;	and place it inside the joints, and under the armpits;
et s’il sent dolor ou porriture en bouelz, et maintes fois avient,	and if there is pain or gangrene in the bowels, and this happens repeatedly,
si les clisterize de vin noir tede, et meismement se li porriture vient jusc’a l’intestine;	if you use black wine enemas, and similarly if the gangrene reaches up to the intestine;
et le perce dedens, et saiches que quant c’est li gros intestines, si est plus legier a saner que li petis.	And insert it within, and know that when it's large intestine, it is easier to heal than the small ones.
Li intestine qui est apelez «jeun» ne puet saner quant il est navrez,	The intestine which is called "juvenile" cannot be healed when it is injured,
et c’est por la planteit des voinnes que i sont, et por la subtiliteit de tout le cors, et l’aprochement de sa nature des ners.	And this is due to the positioning of the veins in them, and due to the subtlety of all the body, and the approach of their nature towards nerves.
Et si li zirbe saut de la plaie, si le remet arrier ausi com l’intestine, tandis qu’il est fres;	And if a boil jumps from the wound, then it should be treated in the same way as an intestine while it is fresh;
et s’il est vielz et devenus vers ou noir, si covient que tu lies le leu qui est noir, que decorremens de sanc n’i viegne,	And if it is old and turned towards or black, then you must tie the part that is black, so that no blood flows from it.
car il i a voinnes et arteres;	for there are veins and arteries;
puis cope ceu qui est entre le liien,	then cut what is between the ligament,
et met les .ij. chiés pendans des la partie desoz la plaie jusque defuer por aligier l’estraction quant li zirbes chiet, et li plaie bowe.	and place both shoulders under part of the over the wound up to beyond it for facilitating the extraction when the ribs are in motion, and the wound is closed.
de la routure dou boueil	of the rupture of the boil
Quant li intestine est rons, et li plaie est petite,	When the intestines are ruptured, and the wound is small,
si la puet on restorer en aucuns homes,	If one can restore it in any way,
por ceu que je vis que uns hons fut navrez ou ventre d’une lance;	because I have seen that a nobleman's or belly was pierced by a lance;
et estoit li plaie au destre de l’estomac,	And the wound was located on the right side of the stomach,
et fut envillie et devint fistule, et en issoit li egestion et li ventositez;	And it became a sinus and turned into a passage for discharge, with both digestion issues and flatulence arising;
je i mis cure selonc ceu que je poi, et ne cessai de subtilier tant qu’il fut sanez, et li leus soudez.	I administered treatment according to what I could do, and didn't stop refining until it was healed, and bound the wounds.
Et quant je le vis souder, je doutai que li malaides n’eust mal en son ventre;	And when I saw them bound, I doubted that the patient might have pain in their belly;
et il n’i ot point de mal, mais demora en millors dispositions, et menjans et bevans;	And there was no harm, but remained in better conditions, eating and drinking;
et dirent aucun experimentors que quant il a petite plaie en l’intestine, qu’il doit estre liiez en teil maniere:	And it was said by some experimenters that when there is a small wound in the intestine, it should be treated in this manner:
pren fremis a grans testes, puis assemble les levres de la plaie,	take large testicles, and then gather the edges of the wound together,
et quant li fremis ait overte la bouche, si la met sus les .ij. levres,	and when the testicles have opened their mouth, place them on the two edges,
si qu’elle estraigne sa bouche sus;	if she forces her mouth up;
et puis li cope la teste, et ce se tient si qu’il ne puet desliier,	and then he holds the head in place so it cannot be released,
puis met .i. autre fremit aprés en celle maniere que devant, tant que li plaie soit toute porprise;	then applies another pressure in this manner as before, until the wound is completely treated;
et cout la plaie.	and finishes the wound.
Cil chief si s’aerdent en l’intestine, et ne vient nulle nuisance au malaide,	Those who are so consumed by the intestines, and cause no harm to the patient,
et se puet on liier l’intestine d’un fil subtil qui est copez de l’intestine d’une beste,	and one can bind the intestine with a fine thread that has been cut from an animal's intestine,
en teil maniere:	in this manner:
pren le chief de cest fil d’intestine que soit mout descharnez,	take this piece of intestines' thread, so that it be from a sheep that is fully digested,
et puis lie au chief de cest fil .i. fil de lin subtil tort,	And then to the head of this thread .i., a fine linen thread twisted,
puis boute le fil en l’aguille, et en cout l’intestine, et le ramoinne en la routure;	then knot the thread in the needle and sew it through the intestine, and reset it at the opening;
et ceste maniere de costure de fremis nen est fuers que selonc la voie de fiance et d’esperance;	and this way of suturing stitches should only follow the path of hope and expectation;
et se li plaie est grans et large, meismement quant elle est en l’un des grailes intestines, si n’i a engien ne santeit, fuer que subtiliteit.	and if the wound is large and broad, especially when it is in one of the large intestines, even without injury or sickness, let there be delicacy.
de fistule ou qu’ele soit	regarding a fistula, or if it exists
Saiches que toute plaie ou aposteme, quant il enveillist, si est apelee universement «fistule»,	Know that every wound or abscess, when it matures, is universally called "fistula",
et meismement quant elle est chevee et rent bowe.	and similarly when it is covered and begins to heal.
Et fistule est selonc la verteit nodation fautree dure et blainche, ou on ne sent dolor,	And a fistula is according to the true nature of the hard, yellowed mass where no pain is felt,
et est ausi chevee com li penne d’un oiseil;	And also as hairy as a bird's feathers;
et aucune fois en saut clere bowe, et autre fois espesse;	And not once clear and smooth, and another time thick and rough;
aucune fois poc, et autre fois assez;	Not always little, and other times sufficient;
et je en ai jai parleit en la division des plaies, que toute plaie que n’est sanee, et il n’i a char,	and I have spoken about the classification of wounds; that every wound that is not healed, and there is no flesh,
ce n’est fuers que par une des .viiij. causes:	It is only through one of the eight causes:
c’est a savoir, par la petitece dou sanc ou cors;	This is to say, due to the weakness or obstruction in blood flow or wounds;
ou por sa malice;	Or because of its inherent wickedness;
ou por ceu qu’il i a char dure dedens, et sus les levres, que n’i laisse naistre char;	or due to the presence of hard flesh within and on the lips that prevents new tissue from forming.
ou il i a trop de bowe;	In this place there is too much blood;
ou li leus est porris, et li matiere est de male qualiteit;	or the veins are swollen, and the substance is of bad quality;
ou li medicine n’est mie bone en la cure;	or the remedy is not good in the treatment;
ou por ceu que li corruption est maniere de pestilence;	or because it resembles a plague;
ou por la proprieteit en la region est tardive li digestion, et tarde li santeit, et enflee par nature;	Because of its property in the area being late, digestion is slow, and recovery is also delayed, and escapes naturally;
ou il i a voinnes ou os:	There are veins or bones:
et j’ai ja mostreit toutes ces causes, et les signes, et les cures de medicines en la division.	and I have shown all these causes, and the signs, and the treatments with medicines in this section.
Or covient que je te faice a savoir la cure de fistule qui est faite par oevre de mains.	So, it is necessary for me to inform you about the treatment of an abscess which is performed by manual work.
Saiches que fistule avient en tous membres dou cors;	Know that a fistula occurs in all limbs of the body;
car il i a fistules que vienent as grans voines, et as arteres, et as ners,	because there are fistulas that come from large veins, and arteries, and nerves,
ou au syfac, ou a l’intestine, ou a la vessie, ou a aucunes des costes,	or at the stomach, or in the intestines, or in the bladder, or in any of the ribs,
ou a l’espinee dou dos, ou a aucune jointe des mains ou des piez;	or in the spine of the back, or in any joint of the hands or feet;
et si a teil que vient a la proprieteit dou membre principeil, et as semblans leus.	And indeed when it comes to acquiring the property of the main limb, and recognizing their characteristics.
Et toutes les fistules que sont de ceste maniere sont de grief sanation, et n’i a fors que labour, et ignorance;	And all the fistulas that are this way require healing, and there is nothing else but labor, and ignorance;
et se il i a aucune fistule que ne veigne mie jusc’a leu que j’ai dit, et tu as fiance de la cure,	and if there is no fistula that does not end up at the one I have said, and you have taken care of the treatment,
et tu la vues conoistre, si pren une tente d’arain ou de fer, se li fistule est droite, si la quier;	and you will know it, if you take an araneus or iron tent, if the fistula is straight, then touch it;
et se li fistule est torte, si la cerche d’une subtil tente de plonc,	And if the fistula is twisted, then one seeks with a fine needle of thread,
car li plons se ploie mues entor la tortuositeit;	for the knots do fold and move within the twists;
et se li fistule a mains pertus et tu ne la pues mie bien cerchier par tentes,	and if the fistula is at awkward angles and you cannot find it well by trying with guesses,
si la clisterize par l’un des pertus,	if you insert the catheter through one of those awkward angles,
car la moistors si cort d’un pertus a autre, et la mundifie;	for moisture can travel from one part to another, and cleanse;
puis la quier saigement a ton pooir, que tu conoisses s’il i a os ou nerf, et est chevee em parfont,	then inquire carefully according to your ability, that you may know if there is bone or nerve, and feel it all around;
et demande bien au malaide de la dolor qu’il sent au presser de ta main, et le leu ou il la sent;	and ask the patient about their pain when you press your hand on them, and where they feel it;
et quant tu savras vraiement le leu ou elle est, et s’elle est loing de jointure, ou de nerf, ou d’artere ou de voine,	and once you know exactly where it is, and if it's far from a joint, or a nerve, or an artery or vein,
ou en aucuns des leus que je t’ai dit, si la cope selonc ceu que je t’ai dit,	In any of those limbs which I have told you about, if one follows as I have told you,
et oste fuer la fautreure et les chars corrumpues que sont dedens;	and for the extraction of bones and decayed organs that are within;
et puis la cure tant qu’elle soit sanee,	and then the treatment until it is healed,
et se li fistule est bien parfonde de droit endroit, si covient que tu copes em parfont, tant com tu pues,	and if the fistula is well dug straight through, you should dig out as far as possible, just as much as you can.
puis i met tentes moillies en medicine ague, et les boute jusc’au chief de la fistule,	Then I mix wet cloths with medicinal water, and immerse them up to the tip of the pus sack.
tant que li medicine corrode la superfluiteit qui est demoree au fons;	As long as the medicine dissolves the excess that has remained at the bottom;
et puis i met oignemens enjanrans sainne char, tant qu’il soit sanez;	And then I cover it with clean bandages until it is healed.
et s’il n’est sanez par ceu, si le cauterize si com nos avons dit,	If it hasn't healed through this method, then apply the cautery as we have explained,
et se li os est corrompus de la fistule, si le cope.	And if the bone is corrupted by the fistula, then he treats it.
Se voinne ou ners ne te greve ou membres principelz, si com nos avons dit;	If a vein or nerve is compressed or affects the main limbs, as we have said;
et se li os est descovers, et il i a corruption et noiror, si lou reis tant que li corruption soit toute ostee,	And if the bone is exposed, and there's corruption and decay, then heal it until all the decay is removed,
puis le cure de choses enjanrans char tant qu’il soit sanez;	Then treat it with various medicines until it becomes healthy;
et s’il n’est sanez, et rent bowe si com devant,	And if it isn't healed, and you guide it back as before,
saiches que tu n’es mie alez jusc’a font:	You should know that you are not quite there just until the mark:
si descuevre et quier tant que tu soies au fons,	if you uncover and desire it, even when you're at the bottom,
et oste toute la corruption, puis restore le leu;	and remove all the decay, then restore its place;
et s’il est ensi sanez, c’est bien.	And if he is thus healthy, this is well.
Se ceu non, saiches que la corruption est trop en parfont, que tu n’i pues avenir;	But if not, know that the corruption is too much in perfection, that you cannot bring it forward;
si n’i a autre engien que dou lassier a nature;	if there is no other way except to let it be done by nature;
et s’il i a i petit os corrumput, et tu le pues traire as tenailles,	and if there's a little corrupt bone and you can remove it with tongs,
si l’estrai a .i. estrument covenauble a ceu,	If you extract with an instrument suitable for this,
et s’il i a maint os, si les trai trestoz, ne n’en laissier nes un;	and if there are many bones, treat them all, do not leave even one;
et se li moistor te fait contraire, et il n’i a error ne paour,	and if moisture opposes this and causes fear or hesitation,
si cope et moistor et char, et delivre les os.	if it is necessary to cut through moisture and flesh, and free the bones.
Et se tu ne les pues oster a une houre, si met sus la plaie chose enjanrant porriture,	And if you cannot remove them within an hour, then place something to combat putrefaction on the wound.
et laisse tant que li leus soit porris entor les os,	and let it be until the bones are rotten inside the flesh,
et adonc si avront plus legierement les os;	then from then on, they will have lighter the bones;
et se c’est uns grans os, si com de jambe ou de cuisse,	and if it's a large bone, like in the leg or thigh,
si reis tant soulement la corruption tant que li noiror soit toute ostee,	if you only release the corruption until all the blackness is removed,
puis restoure la plaie;	then heal the wound;
et s’il en i a grant partie dou corrumput, et vient jusc’a mole de l’os;	and if there's a large part of corruption and it reaches up to the flesh of the bone;
si le covient soier et coper tout jusc’a la corruption, et puis le cure tant qu’il soit soudez;	if it suits, treat and cover up to the area of corruption, and then heal until it is joined together;
et je te dirai d’une fistule qui avint .i. home en sa jambe,	And I will tell you of a case involving a fistula that occurred in one's leg.
si que tu i preignes exemple et aide en ton ovraige.	So that you may take it as an example and gain help in your work.
Il fut .i. jovencelz entor .xxx. ans, qui ot une dolor en sa jambe d’une cause que vint dedens le cors,	There was a young person of around thirty years old who experienced pain in their leg due to an internal cause within the body.
tant que les matieres vinrent a la jambe, et fut enflee d’un gros aposteme, et n’ot point de cause defuer por ovrir;	And as long as the contents reached the leg, it was plagued by a large abscess, and there was no external reason for opening it;
mais li mire par lor folie ovrerent tant sus que li apostemes ovri,	yet they would expose their faces so much that abscesses were opened,
et en corroient mout de matieres, et devint fistule, et i vint mout de pertus que tuit gitoient bowe et moistor dou cors;	and they would corrode some materials, and became a fistula, and much was lost that all complained of pain and the moisture of the body;
et maint mire i mirent cure entor .ij. ans, et n’i ot nul saige en l’art de mains,	and many patients were treated for over two years, and there was no expert in the art of surgery.
tant que je i fui apelez, et vi sa jambe et les medicines dont on le curoit,	as long as I was called upon, and saw his leg and the remedies used to treat him,
et ceu que corroit par les pertus a grant cors;	And that which grows through the narrow passages with great force;
et devenoit rouges li cors dou jouvenceil, et avoit color citrine.	And became red on the cheeks like the color of youth, and had a yellowish tint.
Je boutai une tente en l’un de ces pertus, et puis cerchai toz les pertus,	I set up a tent in one of these narrow passages, and then searched all the passages,
et trovai que li uns venoit encontre l’autre de toutes les parties de la jambe.	and found that some came against each other from all parts of the leg.

et le trovai corrumput et perciet, et venoit li corruption jusc’a l’os dedens;	and found it decayed and perforated, and the corruption was reaching to the interior of the bone;
je soiai ceu qui m’aparissoit de l’os corrumput, et cuidai qu’il n’i eust autre corruption, fuer que celi que je ostai;	I was the one that appeared from the decayed part of the bone, and I thought there was no other decay, only what I had taken out;
et comensai a restourer la plaie de medicines sodans par lonc tens, et ne pot souder;	and began to heal the wound with medication for a long time, but could not stitch it together;
et puis rencomensai, et descovri l’os si com devant,	And then I began again, and exposed the bone as before,
et trovai la corruption continuee en l’os, et la soiai, et puis l’ostai, et me penai de souder le leu;	and found the continuous decay in the bone, and the screw, and then removed it, and bent to焊接 its place;
mais je ne pou tant que je copai entor une palme de l’os, et le traï fuer a tout son mole,	but I could not do that as long as I copied the shape of a palm of the bone, and it was set to its full size,
puis le restourai de medicines; et il fut sanez et soudez hastanment,	then I would treat it with medicine; and it healed and was joined quickly,
et ne covint plus rencomencier l’ovraige fors por la foibleté dou malaide, qui ne pooit soffrir,	And it could not be resumed for lack of strength from the patient, who cannot endure,

Car por l’evacuation sanglotoit sovent, mais il fut sanez entierement,	For during blood loss was common, but it was completely healed,
et nasquit en leu de l’os une char dure, et fut de bone disposition et n’ot point de nuisement ne de contraire dou tout en tout, ne a l’aleir ne a venir.	And in the place of the bone there formed a hard flesh, and it was well arranged and had no harm or opposite from all to all, neither inside nor outside.
Et se li os est brisiez en aucun leu dou cors, si le covient soier en ceste maniere:	And if any bone is broken anywhere in the body, it ought to be treated thus:
pren .i. liien, et l’estrain au chief de l’os qui apert,	take hold of it, and press against the end of the bone that is exposed,
et comande aucun k’il l’estende en haut;	and command him to extend it upwards;
et met .i. autre lien de lainne plus gros dou premier liien, et le lie sus la char qui est desor l’os,	and put another one of thicker thread compared to the first one, and tie it around the tissue that is inside the bone,
et estent le chief, si que tu traies la char corrumpue au desoz,	And if there's pus in the head, so you extract the corrupted flesh at once,
et descuevre la char sus le leu ou tu vues soier, que li soie ne blece la char;	And uncover the flesh on the limb where you see sinew, that the sinew not injure the flesh;
et met .i. tison ou une tauble desoz l’os por mues coper la char corrumpue;	And place one stick or a board over the bone to cover the putrefied flesh;
et covient tant soier com on puet veoir et sentir la corruption, et soier ancor autre fois.	And it should be done as far as one can see and sense the decay, and do it again if necessary.
Et se li os est corrumpus, et n’apert mie, et li corruptions est en mileu ou en une partie,	And if the bone is corrupted, and does not open, and the corruption is in the middle or in a part,

et se li corruptions est en la continuation des .ij. jointes, si n’i a autre angien que dou coper;	And if corruption has spread through both of these joints, there's no other way to fix it besides surgery;
et se li corruptions est ou poignil de la main, ou ou poignil dou piet, si est mout fort celle chose,	And if corruption is in the thumb or forefinger of the hand, or in the heel bone of the foot, such a thing must be done quite forcefully;

et saiches que li incisoire et les soies por coper ces os sont maintes, selonc l’assise des os et l’aparance d’ous,	And know that the surgeon and surgeons who work with these bones are many, according to the position of the bones and their appearance,

si porpense l’estrument dont tu as mestier selonc ceu qu’il le covient.	if you consider the tool that you need according to what is suitable.
dou feu	with fire
Li chiés porrissent ou par cause dedens, ou par cause defuer;	The shoulder joint gets dislocated either from within, or due to heat;
et quant tu avras medicinee celle corrosion par la cure des medicines, et il ne profitent mie,	And when you have healed that corruption through the treatment of the medicines, and they do not benefit at all,
si covient coper celui membre jusques au leu ou li corrosion vient,	Then it is necessary to cover that limb up to its joint where the corruption comes from,
si que li malaides eschaipe par ceu de la mort, ou par la malice, qui est plus grans, de la defaute dou membre;	so that the disease does not escape through death or by malice, which is greater than the fault of the limb;
et li signes si est que li membres devient noir, si qu’il semble qu’il soit ars dou feu,	and if you see these signs, then the limb turns black, as though it has been burned by fire.
et porrist aprés la noiror, puis va celle corrosions de membre em membre,	And after the night, then comes this process of corroding limb by limb,
et prent par tout le cors; si te haste dou coper,	and takes over the entire body; if you hurry with it,

se li corrosion est au chief dou doi, si le cope, et ne li doner mie espaice de venir jusc’a la main.	if it's at the head of two fingers, if you do so, and do not give it space to come up to the hand.
Et s’elle vient jusc’a la main, si la cope a la jointe, si que la corrosion ne viegne jusc’a bras;	And if it comes up to the wrist, if you stop at the joint, so that the disease does not extend up to the elbow;
et s’elle vient au bras, si le cope au coute; et s’elle passe le coute, c’est li mors,	And if it reaches the arm, if surgery is delayed; and if the treatment passes the point of surgical intervention, then many die.
et n’i vaut amenistremens fuers que li quantitez de sa vertut;	And its value can only be determined by the strength of its potency.
et tot ensi fai quant li corrosion vient ou piet: s’elle vient en la premiere jointe, si la cope aprés l’autre jointe;	And do so as follows when the disease reaches or affects a part: if it reaches the first joint, if surgery is performed after another joint;
et s’elle vient ou piet, si cope tout le piet;	And if she comes or a piece, if cut all the piece;
et s’elle monte en la jambe, si cope a la jointure dou genoil;	And if she goes up in the leg, if cut at the knee joint;
et s’elle vient desus le genoil, si n’i a autre engien que dou lassier le malaide a mort;	And if she comes above the knee, there's no other way than to make the patient die by killing the limb.
et li maniere dou coper ou dou soier le membre si est que tu le lie desus et desoz,	The method of fixing or securing a member is that you bind it above and below,
et estende uns menistres l’un des liiens aval, et uns autres ministres l’autre liien amont,	And extend one surgeon to the lower ligament, and another surgeon to the upper ligament above.

et je te conterai k’il avint a .i. home en som piet:	and I will tell you what happened at one man's house in my book:
il li avint une noiror qui sembloit arsure de feu,	He had a black mark that seemed to be like an ember of fire,

car li vertus de l’ome estoit foible; et il se despera toz, et revint en sa terre,	because the power of the medicine was weak; and he completely lost hope, and returned to his home,
et se hasta de coper sa main, et fut sanez;	And if they raise their hand, and are well.

Aucune fois vient aposteme en leu charnut, et demore si longement qu’il fait grant assemblee de bowe;	No abscess ever comes to the inner flesh, and stays so long as to cause a large collection of pus;

et li cuir qui est desus est ausi subtilz com .i. drapelz deliiez,	And the skin above is as delicate as one linen sheet,
et ne corront mie jusc’a l’os, ne jusc’au nerf, et telz maladie si est apelee «sain»,	and does not extend up to the bone or to the nerve, and such illnesses are called "blind" or "unknown",
et n’est mie apelee «fistule»;	and is not called "fistula";

Et se tu as fiance que li cuirs s’aerde, et li corruption n’est mie en parfont,	And if you've noticed that the skin is heating up and there's no decay,

adonques le clisterize de medicine egiptiaine qui est ensi faite:	Then use an Egyptian enema medicine which is prepared here:
prenez aisil, et oile, et litargire, igalment, et metez cuire en .i. vassel au feu,	Take arsenic, oil, and litharge, equally, and cook them in a single vessel on the fire,

et aucune fois est clisterizeis d’aigue de cendres,	And never made to be lanced with water from ashes,

Des vers qui naissent entre cuir et char	Worms that are born between the skin and flesh

De la dolor qui vient de ventositeit	Of the pain that comes from wind disturbance
